text-color" title="Authorization">Authorization</h1></div></div><div class="_markdown-container_txmk1_1 mb-8"><div class="markdown-body remark-mdx"><section data-first="true">OAuth is a widely adopted authorization framework that allows you to consent to an App interacting with another on your behalf without having to reveal Merchant&#x27;s sensitive data, such as passwords.</section><section>If you are building integrations that require access to Salla on behalf of other Salla Merchants, you should utilize <a href="https://salla.dev/blog/oauth-2-0-in-action-with-salla/" title="" data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/oauth-2-0-in-action-with-salla/" target="_blank">OAuth 2.0 Protocol for Salla</a>. You can use OAuth in gaining access to Merchants&#x27; stores with either <a href="https://salla.dev/blog/oauth-2-0-in-action-with-salla/" title="" data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/oauth-2-0-in-action-with-salla/" target="_blank">Easy Mode</a> or <a href="https://salla.dev/blog/oauth-2-0-in-action-with-salla/" title="" data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/oauth-2-0-in-action-with-salla/" target="_blank">Custom Mode</a>, using access tokens via the Apps built on <a href="https://salla.partners/" title="" data-href="https://salla.partners/" target="_blank">Salla Partners Portal</a>, which will be published on<br/><a href="http://apps.salla.sa/" title="" data-href="http://apps.salla.sa/" target="_blank">Salla App Store</a>.</section><div class="markdown-child-root flex admonition admonition-check" data-markdown-component="x-admonition"><div class="flex-0 admonition-title admonition-title-check" style="line-height:24px;width:24px;height:24px"><span role="img" class="appicon app_icon mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M883.498667 225.834667a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1 0 60.330666l-469.333334 469.333334a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1-60.330666 0l-213.333334-213.333334a42.666667 42.666667 0 1 1 60.330667-60.330666L384 665.002667 823.168 225.834667a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1 60.330667 0z"></path></svg></span></div><div class="markdown-child-root flex-1"><section data-first="true" data-last="true"><strong data-first="true">Salla OAuth Format</strong><br/>All calls to the Merchant Public APIs require an Authorization header in this format:<br/><strong>Authorization:</strong> Bearer <code data-last="true">&lt;ACCESS_TOKEN&gt;</code></section></div></div><h1 id="what-you-will-need-before-you-start" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">What You will Need Before You Start:<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#what-you-will-need-before-you-start"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h1><div class="w-full" data-markdown-component="x-steps-container"><div class="ui-steps ui-steps-vertical"><div class="ui-steps-item ui-steps-item-process class="_index_ov9a1_7">1</span></span></div><div class="ui-steps-item-content"><div class="ui-steps-item-title">First Step</div><div class="ui-steps-item-description"><div Partners</a>.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="ui-steps-item ui-steps-item-process ui-steps-item-custom"><div class="ui-steps-item-container"><div class="ui-steps-item-tail"></div><div class="ui-steps-item-icon"><span class="ui-steps-icon"><span class="_index_ov9a1_7">2</span></span></div><div class="ui-steps-item-content"><div class="ui-steps-item-title">Second Step</div><div data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/create-your-first-app-on-salla-developer-portal/" target="_blank">created</a> previously or build a new one from the scratch.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="ui-steps-item ui-steps-item-process ui-steps-item-custom"><div class="ui-steps-item-container"><div class="ui-steps-item-tail"></div><div class="ui-steps-item-icon"><span class="ui-steps-icon"><span class="_index_ov9a1_7">3</span></span></div><div class="ui-steps-item-content"><div class="ui-steps-item-title">Third Step</div><div class="ui-steps-item-description"><div class="markdown-child-root">Choose an OAuth method, <a href="https://salladev.hashnode.dev/review-on-salla-merchants-apis#heading-generate-access-token-using-salla-app-and-demo-store" title="" data-href="https://salladev.hashnode.dev/review-on-salla-merchants-apis#heading-generate-access-token-using-salla-app-and-demo-store" target="_blank">Easy Mode</a> or Custom Mode Authorization.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="ui-steps-item ui-steps-item-process ui-steps-item-custom"><div class="ui-steps-item-container"><div class="ui-steps-item-tail"></div><div class="ui-steps-item-icon"><span class="ui-steps-icon"><span class="_index_ov9a1_7">4</span></span></div><div class="ui-steps-item-content"><div class="ui-steps-item-title">Fourth Step</div><div class="ui-steps-item-description"><div class="markdown-child-root">Set up the scopes of your App to specify the needed access level.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="ui-steps-item data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/how-to-test-your-app-using-salla-demo-stores/" target="_blank">demo store</a>, so no sensitive data is compromised.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="ui-steps-item ui-steps-item-process ui-steps-item-custom"><div class="ui-steps-item-container"><div class="ui-steps-item-tail"></div><div class="ui-steps-item-icon"><span class="ui-steps-icon"><span class="_index_ov9a1_7">6</span></span></div><div class="ui-steps-item-content"><div class="ui-steps-item-title">Sixth Step</div><div class="ui-steps-item-description"><div class="markdown-child-root"><a href="https://salla.dev/blog/how-to-test-your-app-using-salla-demo-stores/" title="" data-first="true" data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/how-to-test-your-app-using-salla-demo-stores/" target="_blank">Install</a> the App on the demo store for real-world mockup test.</div></div></div></div></div></div></div><h1 id="salla-oauth-benefits" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Salla OAuth Benefits<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#salla-oauth-benefits"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h1><div class="_cardGroup_o6dzj_70" data-markdown-component="x-card-group" style="grid-template-columns:repeat(3, minmax(0, 1fr))"><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card" data-first="true"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40">ðŸ” Authorized Access</div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">Apps are given authorized access, which means they can only access resources that the Merchant has authenticated.</span></div></div><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40">â›“ï¸â€ðŸ’¥ Revoke Access</div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">The App&#x27;s authorized access can be revoked at any time by the Merchant by disconnecting the App from the dashboard on Salla Partners.</span></div></div><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card" data-last="true"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40">âŒ›ï¸ Time Limit</div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">OAuth 2.0 access tokens have a time limit. Merchant data will be compromised only until the access token is valid if the App encounters a security breach.</span></div></div></div><h1 id="sallas-oauth20-flow" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Sallaâ€™s OAuth2.0 Flow<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#sallas-oauth20-flow"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h1><section>The <strong>OAuth 2.0</strong> authorization flow is the <strong>initial step in installing an App on the Salla platform</strong>. By requiring the merchant to grant permission for the App to access their data within specific scope, this process helps to ensure that the store&#x27;s data is safe and private. The OAuth 2.0 authorization procedure can be started by one of the following URLs:</section><div class="_cardGroup_o6dzj_70" data-markdown-component="x-card-group" style="grid-template-columns:repeat(2, minmax(0, 1fr))"><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card" data-first="true"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40"></div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">The Authorization URL: <span data-last="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"> <code>https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/auth</code> </span></span></span></div></div><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card" data-last="true"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40"></div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">The Installation URL: <span data-last="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"> <code>https://s.salla.sa/apps/install/{app-id}</code> </span></span></span></div></div></div><h2 id="the-authorization-flow" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">The authorization Flow<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#the-authorization-flow"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h2><section>The <strong>OAuth 2.0</strong> authentication flow for <em>installing an App on a Salla Store</em> includes crucial URLs and endpoints that enable permission granting, code-to-token exchange, redirection, and token refreshing. The process involves the merchant&#x27;s redirection to the <strong>Salla Authorization Server</strong>, login, granting permission, and obtaining an access token for API requests and accessing store data.</section><section>The following table summarize these and endpoints:</section><table><thead><tr class=""><th>URL</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class=""><td>Authorization Endpoint</td><td><span data-index="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"> <code>https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/auth</code> </span></span> <br/> This URL initiates the process of obtaining the merchant&#x27;s permission for the App to access their store data on Salla.</td></tr><tr class=""><td>Token Endpoint</td><td><span data-index="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"> <code>https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/token</code> </span></span> <br/> After the merchant grants permission, the App exchanges the authorization code for an access token at this endpoint.</td></tr><tr class=""><td>Redirect URI</td><td><span data-index="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">https://client-app.com/callback</code></span></span> <br/> Once the authentication process is complete, the authorization server redirects the user&#x27;s browser to the registered redirect URI.</td></tr><tr class=""><td>Refresh Token Endpoint</td><td><span data-index="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"> <code>https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/token</code> </span></span> <br/> If a refresh token is granted, this endpoint allows the client to obtain a new access token when the current one expires.</td></tr><tr class=""><td>User Info Endpoint</td><td><span data-index="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/user/info</code></span></span> <br/> Once the authentication process is completed successfully, the Merchant details can be received via <a href="/5394260e0" title="" data-href="/5394260e0" data-discover="true">this endpoint</a>.</td></tr></tbody></table><div class="markdown-child-root flex admonition admonition-tip" data-markdown-component="x-admonition"><div class="flex-0 admonition-title admonition-title-tip" style="line-height:24px;width:24px;height:24px"><span role="img" class="appicon app_icon mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M375.466667 874.666667c0 12.8 4.266667 21.333333 8.533333 34.133333l29.866667 46.933333c8.533333 12.8 29.866667 25.6 46.933333 25.6h115.2c17.066667 0 38.4-12.8 46.933333-25.6l29.866667-46.933333c4.266667-8.533333 8.533333-21.333333 8.533333-34.133333v-72.533334H375.466667v72.533334zM494.933333 187.733333C413.866667 187.733333 345.6 256 345.6 337.066667c0 17.066667 12.8 29.866667 29.866667 29.866666 17.066667 0 29.866667-12.8 29.866666-29.866666 0-46.933333 38.4-89.6 89.6-89.6 17.066667 0 29.866667-12.8 29.866667-29.866667 0-17.066667-17.066667-29.866667-29.866667-29.866667z"></path><path d="M524.8 42.666667C337.066667 42.666667 200.533333 196.266667 200.533333 362.666667c0 81.066667 29.866667 153.6 81.066667 213.333333 29.866667 34.133333 76.8 106.666667 93.866667 166.4h294.4c17.066667-59.733333 64-132.266667 93.866666-166.4 51.2-55.466667 81.066667-128 81.066667-213.333333 0-174.933333-145.066667-320-320-320z m174.933333 477.866666c-29.866667 34.133333-64 85.333333-89.6 140.8h-174.933333c-25.6-55.466667-59.733333-106.666667-89.6-140.8-38.4-42.666667-59.733333-98.133333-59.733333-157.866666C285.866667 247.466667 375.466667 128 520.533333 128c132.266667 0 234.666667 106.666667 234.666667 234.666667 4.266667 59.733333-17.066667 115.2-55.466667 157.866666z"></path></svg></span></div><div class="markdown-child-root flex-1"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">To use the Authorization Endpoint <strong><span data-index="true" data-last="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><a href="https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/auth" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" data-href="https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/auth" target="_blank">https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/auth</a></span></span></strong> in your code, you will typically need to make an HTTP request to that URL.</section></div></div><section>In addition to the base URLs mentioned above, <strong>OAuth 2.0 also uses query parameters</strong> to pass information during the authentication process. These query parameters serve different purposes and are included in the URLs when making requests to the authorization and token endpoints. Here are some common query parameters used in OAuth 2.0:</section><table><thead><tr class=""><th>Query Parameter</th><th>Description</th><th>Example</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">client_id</code></td><td>Identifies the client application making the request, which values can be fetched from your application on the Salla Partners Portal.</td><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">1311508470xxx</code></td></tr><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">client_secret</code></td><td>Identifies the client application making the request, which values can be fetched from your application on the Salla Partners Portal.</td><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">362985662xxx</code></td></tr><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">response_type</code></td><td>Specifies the desired response type from the authorization server.</td><td><span data-index="true" data-last="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">code</code></span></span></td></tr><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">redirect_uri</code></td><td>Indicates the URI for user redirection after completing the authorization process.</td><td><span data-index="true" data-last="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><a href="https://your-app.com/callback-url" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" data-href="https://your-app.com/callback-url" target="_blank">https://your-app.com/callback-url</a></span></span></td></tr><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">scope</code></td><td>Specifies the requested permissions or access levels.</td><td><span data-index="true" data-last="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">offline_access</code></span></span></td></tr><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">state</code></td><td>Used to maintain state between the authorization request and the callback to prevent cross-site request forgery attacks.</td><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">1234xxxx</code></td></tr><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">code</code></td><td>The authorization code returned by the authorization endpoint.</td><td>xxxxxxxx</td></tr><tr class=""><td><code data-first="true" data-last="true">grant_type</code></td><td>Specifies the type of grant being used to authenticate the client.</td><td><span data-index="true" data-last="true"><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">authorization_code</code></span></span></td></tr></tbody></table><div class="markdown-child-root _container_xe456_1"><h4 id="including-the-client-id-as-a-query-parameter" data-first="true" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Including the client ID as a query parameter<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#including-the-client-id-as-a-query-parameter"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h4><section>It is common practice <strong>to include the client ID as a query parameter in the authorization URL</strong> for OAuth 2.0 authentication. This inclusion allows the authorization server <em>to associate the authentication request with the specific client</em>, ensuring client identification and authentication during the process. Here&#x27;s an example of how the client ID can be included in the authorization URL:</section><span><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><div class="markdown-code-block" data-first="true" data-last="true"><div class="_code_1kvbn_1 relative _container_1kvbn_15 _container-dark_1kvbn_18"><pre class="theme-github-dark _code-block_1kvbn_1 code-block-custom" style="--markdown-x-component-gap:0px"><code class="_code_1kvbn_1 hljs hljs-json">https<span class="hljs-punctuation">:</span><span class="hljs-comment">//accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/auth?client_id=your_client_id&amp;response_type=code&amp;redirect_uri=https://client-app.com/callback&amp;scope=read write&amp;state=random_value</span></code></pre></div></div></span></span><section>In the example above, <code>client_id=your_client_id</code> is appended to the authorization URL, where <em>your_client_id</em> should be replaced with the actual client ID issued by the authorization server.</section><div class="markdown-child-root flex admonition admonition-check" data-markdown-component="x-admonition" data-last="true"><div class="flex-0 admonition-title admonition-title-check" style="line-height:24px;width:24px;height:24px"><span role="img" class="appicon app_icon mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M883.498667 225.834667a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1 0 60.330666l-469.333334 469.333334a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1-60.330666 0l-213.333334-213.333334a42.666667 42.666667 0 1 1 60.330667-60.330666L384 665.002667 823.168 225.834667a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1 60.330667 0z"></path></svg></span></div><div class="markdown-child-root flex-1"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">Including the <strong>client ID as a query parameter</strong> in the authorization URL ensures authentication and identification of the client during <strong>OAuth 2.0</strong>. <em>If the App has been previously approved</em>, <em>scope approval steps may be skipped</em>, streamlining the process.</section></div></div></div><h2 id="the-installation-url" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">The installation URL<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#the-installation-url"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h2><section>On the other hand, <strong>the installation URL</strong> allows for the immediate installation of the App to the merchant store. Unlike the typical authorization URL, the installation URL simplifies the app installation process by providing a direct URL with the <code>app-id</code> as a parameter. This URL can be used to initiate the app installation process. When the merchant clicks on the installation URL, the App will be automatically installed into their Salla Store.</section><section>The following diagram explains the flow of OAuth 2.0 in Salla, which will eventually result in access token generation.</section><section><img src="https://cdn.salla.network/docs/MerchantAPI/Intro-Auth-04.jpeg" alt="OAuth" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" loading="lazy" class=""/></section><h1 id="types-of-oauth-20-in-salla" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Types of OAuth 2.0 in Salla<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#types-of-oauth-20-in-salla"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h1><section>On <a href="https://salla.partners/" title="" data-href="https://salla.partners/" target="_blank">Salla Partners Portal</a>, and when you are creating your <a href="https://salla.dev/blog/create-your-first-app-on-salla-developer-portal/" title="" data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/create-your-first-app-on-salla-developer-portal/" target="_blank">App</a>, inside the App page details within the App Keys section, you will be provided with two methods for the OAuth protocol:</section><div data-type="list" class="markdown-child-root"><div data-type="list-item" data-index="0" data-orderer="false" class="markdown-child-root flex" data-first="true"><div class="_unOrderContainer_1v6rr_18"><div class="_dash_1v6rr_28"></div></div><div class="markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true"><strong data-first="true">Easy Mode</strong>, which is a simplified version of the protocol that requires minimal setup.</section></div></div><div data-type="list-item" data-index="1" data-orderer="false" class="markdown-child-root flex" data-last="true"><div class="_unOrderContainer_1v6rr_18"><div class="_dash_1v6rr_28"></div></div><div class="markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true"><strong data-first="true">Custom Mode</strong>, which allows for more advanced, manual configuration and the use of callback URLs.</section></div></div></div><section><img src="https://cdn.salla.network/docs/MerchantAPI/Intro-Auth-05.png?v" alt="Modes Image" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" loading="lazy" class=""/></section><h2 id="easy-mode-recommended" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Easy Mode (Recommended)<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#easy-mode-recommended"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h2><section>One of the foremost options of authorization via OAuth 2.0 in <a href="https://salla.partners" title="" data-href="https://salla.partners" target="_blank">Salla Partners</a> is Easy Mode Authorization. Utilizing Sallaâ€™s easy mode option, you can get the â€œ<a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413#app-store-authorize" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413#app-store-authorize" target="_blank">access token</a>â€ in one step automatically. It allows you to listen to the event, <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413#app-store-authorize" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413#app-store-authorize" target="_blank"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">app.store.authorize</code></a>, and then the process of generating the â€œ<a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413#app-store-authorize" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413#app-store-authorize" target="_blank">access token</a>â€ will be handled automatically at Sallaâ€˜s side back to you via the <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421119#set-up-troubleshooting-environment" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421119#set-up-troubleshooting-environment" target="_blank">Webhook URL</a> specified in the Webhooks/Notifications your of your App.</section><section>By selecting the Easy Mode Authorization option, Salla will handle everything, including extracting the authorization code and providing the client id and secret key together with the auth code to generate an access token. In the end, you will receive all of the above data in the form of a payload that contains a new access token generated for you, <strong>as the life validity of access tokens with Salla is 2 weeks</strong>.</section><div class="markdown-child-root flex admonition admonition-check" data-markdown-component="x-admonition"><div class="flex-0 admonition-title admonition-title-check" style="line-height:24px;width:24px;height:24px"><span role="img" class="appicon app_icon mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M883.498667 225.834667a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1 0 60.330666l-469.333334 469.333334a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1-60.330666 0l-213.333334-213.333334a42.666667 42.666667 0 1 1 60.330667-60.330666L384 665.002667 823.168 225.834667a42.666667 42.666667 0 0 1 60.330667 0z"></path></svg></span></div><div class="markdown-child-root flex-1"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">Find more on how to further setup the easy mode by reading <a href="https://salladev.hashnode.dev/review-on-salla-merchants-apis#heading-generate-access-token-using-salla-app-and-demo-store" title="" using a Salla App where both are linked to your Partners Account .</section><div class="w-full" data-markdown-component="x-steps-container"><div class="ui-steps ui-steps-vertical"><div for the App.<section data-last="true"><img class="ui-steps-item-content"><div class="ui-steps-item-title">Install App using Demo Stores</div><div class="ui-steps-item-description"><div class="markdown-child-root">Scroll down to the Test App store dashboard page where you can approve the App installment. Approve the installment request to proceed.<section data-last="true"><img src="https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdkw7LCQhjDa4L4P7DcPpKjFBz1tUZbASmPw031UgvU6fEZ6I3PTHzjSosWJiND0nwaZtCRArYTZXz9If3nZteMEQ6OPpzsS1Csp-XYmAtYaKgMt54uiqT9TFinWtEQvrYGS3sD-ekmiCtPHqB9zI9Ig4Jx?key=z6sib4CQioMEBm7IjT__cQ" class="ui-steps-item-content"><div class="ui-steps-item-title">Retrieve Access Token from Webhook</div><div class="ui-steps-item-description"><div class="markdown-child-root">After that, go back to the <a href="http://Webhook.site" title="" data-href="http://Webhook.site" target="_blank">Webhook.site</a> and get the Access Token from the <code>app.store.authorize</code> event.<section data-last="true"><img src="https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXdhWejEXoVP2Q0sSfhsYkG4h9oZPja9n_e_b-u8gE_3Mo8ZI8DGe0L-Y-9KoMiCyYI8rkp84VhT5b6B6txXyyN3hp3iAoRRfUxrYpGVBUOoUD0Xd9SEvjQBsRM5CZR1bh2Wjs2Dwklq7q8Z6A__l-V1Ef8?key=z6sib4CQioMEBm7IjT__cQ" alt="" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" loading="lazy" class=""/></section></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><br/><div class="markdown-child-root admonition admonition-tip" data-markdown-component="x-admonition"><div class="admonition-title admonition-title-tip" style="margin-bottom:4px"><span role="img" class="appicon app_icon mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M375.466667 874.666667c0 12.8 4.266667 21.333333 8.533333 93.866666-166.4 51.2-55.466667 81.066667-128 81.066667-213.333333 0-174.933333-145.066667-320-320-320z m174.933333 477.866666c-29.866667 34.133333-64 85.333333-89.6 106.666667 234.666667 234.666667 4.266667 59.733333-17.066667 115.2-55.466667 157.866666z"></path></svg></span>App Update</div><div class="pl-6 markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">In the easy mode, when the Merchant updates the app, Salla sends you the <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413?nav=01HNA8M216X4HFNGWM9TWSTCKQ" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413?nav=01HNA8M216X4HFNGWM9TWSTCKQ" target="_blank"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">app.updated</code></a> event. After that, Salla sends you the <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413?nav=01HNA8M216X4HFNGWM9TWSTCKQ" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421413?nav=01HNA8M216X4HFNGWM9TWSTCKQ" target="_blank"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">app store.authorized</code></a> event, which provides you with the new access token and refresh token. This information will be delivered to you via webhook. Accordingly, you are required to update the access token and refresh token in your database.</section></div></div><div class="markdown-child-root admonition admonition-warning" data-markdown-component="x-admonition"><div class="admonition-title admonition-title-warning" style="margin-bottom:4px"><span role="img" class="appicon app_icon mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M449.216 54.72a128 128 0 0 1 172.16 45.184l0.192 0.192 361.344 603.328 0.384 0.576a128 128 0 0 1-109.44 192H150.144a128 128 0 0 1-109.44-192l0.32-0.64L402.56 99.84a128 128 0 0 1 46.656-45.12z m62.72 68.864a42.688 42.688 0 0 0-36.352 20.48l-361.152 602.88a42.688 42.688 0 0 0 36.48 63.744h722.176a42.624 42.624 0 0 0 36.48-63.744L548.48 144.128a42.688 42.688 0 0 0-36.48-20.48z m0 175.104c23.68 0 42.752 19.072 42.752 42.624V512a42.688 42.688 0 1 1-85.376 0V341.312c0-23.552 19.136-42.624 42.688-42.624z m-42.624 384c0-23.552 19.136-42.688 42.688-42.688h0.448a42.688 42.688 0 0 1 0 85.312H512a42.688 42.688 0 0 1-42.688-42.624z"></path></svg></span>WARNING</div><div class="pl-6 markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">The <code>expires</code> variable is returned as a unix timestamp value for the app event <code>app.store.authorize</code>.</section></div></div><h2 id="custom-mode" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Custom Mode<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#custom-mode"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h2><section>When implementing an OAuth flow or any other third-party API that needs to redirect to the App after authentication or authorization, a callback URL should be set. The App will use this URL to reroute back to the App after the login and App scopes&#x27; permission procedures are finished. This cycle of authentication is called Custom Mode authentication.</section><h3 id="custom-mode-use-cases" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Custom Mode Use Cases:<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#custom-mode-use-cases"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h3><div class="_cardGroup_o6dzj_70" data-markdown-component="x-card-group" style="grid-template-columns:repeat(3, minmax(0, 1fr))"><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card" data-first="true"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40"></div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">App for online grocery stores that redirect users back to the store after they log in with their Google account.</span></div></div><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40"></div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">App for onlines store that redirects customers back to the product page after they sign up for a newsletter</span></div></div><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card" data-last="true"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40"></div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">App for bookstores that redirects customers back to their reading list after they rate a book.</span></div></div></div><section>There are two steps that we need to follow in order to successfully set up a Custom Mode OAuth in Salla:</section><h3 id="1-user-authorization" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">1. User Authorization<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#1-user-authorization"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h3><section>A Merchant has to authorize your App, with the set of App scopes, to be able to proceed with the process of obtaining the access token. Direct the Merchant to the callback URL you used while setting up your App on <a href="https://salla.partners" title="" data-href="https://salla.partners" target="_blank">Salla Partner Portal</a>. If this is the first time that you are requesting authorization from a Merchant, the merchant will be asked to log in to his/her Salla Store.</section><section>To obtain the access token for your App, the Merchant needs to authorize it with the App scopes.<br/>Once the Merchant has logged in to their Salla Store account, they will be prompted by Salla to authorize access to your App. The merchant will be asked to grant authorization for your App to access their store data with the defined scopes.</section><section><img src="https://cdn.salla.network/docs/MerchantAPI/Intro-Auth-01-02.png" alt="Intro to OAuth image" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" loading="lazy" class=""/></section><br/><section>If the access has been authorized, the user will be redirected to the Callback URL with the authorization code in the code query parameter, which you can fetch to continue the process of obtaining the access token:</section><span><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><code data-first="true" data-last="true">https://yourapp.com/callback?code={code-value}&amp;scope={app-scopes}+offline_access&amp;state={state-value}
</code></span></span><h3 id="2-access-token-generation" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">2. Access Token Generation<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#2-access-token-generation"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h3><section>When the Merchant authorizes the App, Salla returns the Merchant to your Callback URL with a code parameter containing an authorization code. Use the code in your access token request, which is a <code>POST</code> request with the required parameters to the token endpoint.</section><div data-markdown-component="x-tabs-container"><div class="ui-tabs ui-tabs-top ui-tabs-full-content ui-tabs-full-content--scrollable"><div role="tablist" class="ui-tabs-nav"><div class="ui-tabs-nav-wrap" style="flex-grow:1"><div tabindex="0">Access Token Request</div></div><div data-node-key=".$1" class="ui-tabs-tab"><div role="tab" aria-selected="false" class="ui-tabs-tab-btn" tabindex="0">Access Token Response</div></div><div class="ui-tabs-ink-bar"></div></div></div><div class="ui-tabs-nav-operations ui-tabs-nav-operations-hidden" style="flex-grow:1"><button type="button" class="ui-tabs-nav-more" style="visibility:hidden;order:1" tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-controls="null-more-popup" id="null-more" aria-expanded="false"><span role="img" aria-label="ellipsis" class="ui-tabs-content ui-tabs-content-top"><div role="tabpanel" tabindex="0" aria-hidden="false" class="ui-tabs-tabpane ui-tabs-tabpane-active"><div class="markdown-child-root">Easily run the request straight from Postman by providing the required data to generate an access token<section><br data-first="true"/> <a mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M449.216 54.72a128 128 0 0 1 172.16 45.184l0.192 0.192 361.344 603.328 0.384 0.576a128 128 0 0 1-109.44 192H150.144a128 128 0 0 1-109.44-192l0.32-0.64L402.56 99.84a128 128 0 0 1 46.656-45.12z m62.72 68.864a42.688 42.688 0 0 0-36.352 1-42.688-42.624z"></path></svg></span>WARNING</div><div class="pl-6 markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">Easy Mode is the only way allowed for published apps on the <a href="https://apps.salla.sa" title="" data-href="https://apps.salla.sa" target="_blank">Salla App Store</a>. Since Postman uses custom mode, you can implement that in your app for testing purposes only.</section></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="body-definition" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Body Definition<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#body-definition"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h3><section>The following enlists the values that are sent to the User Authorization endpoint to generate an access token:</section><div data-markdown-component="x-dataschema-container"><div class="ui-card ui-card-bordered ui-card-small _parameters__card_1gs08_12"><div class="ui-card-head"><div class="ui-card-head-wrapper"><div class="ui-card-head-title">AccessToken</div></div></div><div class="ui-card-body"><div class="pl-4"><div class="flex items-center justify-center p-12"><div class="ui-skeleton ui-skeleton-active"><div class="ui-skeleton-content"><h3 class="ui-skeleton-title" style="width:38%"></h3><ul class="ui-skeleton-paragraph"><li></li><li></li><li style="width:61%"></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><br/><div class="markdown-highlight markdown-highlight-gray" data-markdown-component="x-highlight"><div class="flex"><section class="markdown-child-root flex-1" style="width:fit-content;word-break:break-word;padding:0;margin-top:0;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:8px"><section data-first="true"><h3 data-first="true" data-last="true" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Important Notes<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#undefined"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h3></section><table data-last="true"><thead><tr class=""><th></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class=""><td>â€¢ Access tokens expire after 2 weeks (14 days).</td></tr><tr class=""><td>â€¢ If you want to generate the refresh token, set the scope value as <code>offline_access</code>. E.G: <code>scope = offline_access</code>.</td></tr><tr class=""><td>â€¢ The <code>expires</code> variable is returned as <code>seconds</code> timestamp value</td></tr><tr class=""><td>â€¢ Upon obtaining the access token, developers can utilize the <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/api-5394260" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/api-5394260" target="_blank">User Info endpoint</a> URL, <code>https://accounts.salla.sa/oauth2/user/info</code>, to retrieve the Merchant details and store them alongside the access tokens.</td></tr></tbody></table></section></div></div><h3 id="refresh-access-token" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Refresh Access Token<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#refresh-access-token"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h3><section>A typical reason for refreshing a token is that the original access token has expired, which lasts for only 14 days (2 weeks). If you would like to request a new access token, you may do so by sending Sallaâ€™s authorization server a token refresh request. Refresh tokens are single-use only, meaning they become invalid after the first use.</section><section>Every time a developer uses a refresh token to request a new access token, a new refresh token is issued, and the previous token is invalidated. This mechanism adds an extra layer of security, making it more difficult for attackers to use stolen refresh tokens. A refresh token lasts for 1 month, and attempting to use it twice invalidates the associated access token.</section><div class="markdown-child-root admonition admonition-danger" data-markdown-component="x-admonition"><div class="admonition-title admonition-title-danger" style="margin-bottom:4px"><span role="img" class="appicon app_icon mr-2" style="font-size:16px"><svg viewBox="0 0 1024 1024" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" role="img"><path d="M512 128a384 384 0 1 0 0 768A384 384 0 0 0 512 128zM42.688 512a469.312 469.312 0 1 1 938.624 0A469.312 469.312 0 0 1 42.688 512zM353.856 353.92c16.64-16.64 43.648-16.64 60.288 0L512 451.648 609.856 353.92a42.688 42.688 0 1 1 60.288 60.288l-97.792 97.92 97.792 97.792a42.688 42.688 0 1 1-60.288 60.352L512 572.288l-97.856 97.92a42.688 42.688 0 0 1-60.288-60.352L451.648 512 353.92 414.144a42.688 42.688 0 0 1 0-60.288z"></path></svg></span>Warning: Refresh Token Reuse</div><div class="pl-6 markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true">Reusing refresh tokens in parallel processes or making multiple simultaneous refresh requests can lead to complete authentication failure. When a refresh token is used more than once, Salla&#x27;s OAuth server will:</section><div data-type="list" class="markdown-child-root"><div data-type="list-item" data-index="0" data-orderer="false" class="markdown-child-root flex" data-first="true"><div class="_unOrderContainer_1v6rr_18"><div class="_dash_1v6rr_28"></div></div><div class="markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">Invalidate the refresh token</section></div></div><div data-type="list-item" data-index="1" data-orderer="false" class="markdown-child-root flex"><div class="_unOrderContainer_1v6rr_18"><div class="_dash_1v6rr_28"></div></div><div class="markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">Revoke all access tokens obtained with it</section></div></div><div data-type="list-item" data-index="2" data-orderer="false" class="markdown-child-root flex"><div class="_unOrderContainer_1v6rr_18"><div class="_dash_1v6rr_28"></div></div><div class="markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">Reject all subsequent authentication attempts using that refresh token</section></div></div><div data-type="list-item" data-index="3" data-orderer="false" class="markdown-child-root flex" data-last="true"><div class="_unOrderContainer_1v6rr_18"><div class="_dash_1v6rr_28"></div></div><div class="markdown-child-root"><section data-first="true" data-last="true">Requires the Merchant to reinstall the application from the <a href="https://apps.salla.sa" title="" data-href="https://apps.salla.sa" target="_blank">Salla App Store</a> for you to regain access to their data.</section></div></div></div><section>This security measure is implemented in accordance with <a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc6819#section-5.2.2.3" title="" data-href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc6819#section-5.2.2.3" target="_blank">RFC 6819 Section 5.2.2.3</a> to prevent replay attacks.</section><div class="_TipContainer_chsr3_1" data-first="true" data-last="true"><div class="flex items-center pl-1"><div class="relative mr-4 w-4 h-4 rounded-full text-white flex items-center justify-center"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="scale:calc(24 / 20);margin-bottom:2px"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M10 2C4.47715 2 0 6.47715 0 12C0 17.5228 4.47715 22 10 22C15.5228 22 20 17.5228 20 12C20 6.47715 15.5228 2 10 2ZM14.7337 9.91555C15.0888 9.56053 15.0888 8.98493 14.7337 8.6299C14.3787 8.27488 13.8031 8.27488 13.4481 8.6299L8.63636 13.4416L6.55192 11.3572C6.19689 11.0022 5.62129 11.0022 5.26627 11.3572C4.91124 11.7122 4.91124 12.2878 5.26627 12.6428L7.99354 15.3701C8.34856 15.7251 8.92417 15.7251 9.27919 15.3701L14.7337 9.91555Z" fill="var(--ui-green-6)"></path></svg><div class="absolute top-full mt-1 rounded-full" style="width:1px;background-color:var(--ui-green-2);left:0.46875rem;height:calc(var(--markdown-x-component-gap) + 0px);top:calc(var(--markdown-x-component-gap) + 1px)"></div></div><div class="m-0 flex-1 text-base font-semibold text-slate-900 dark:text-slate-200 markdown-child-root"> <strong>Recommended Implementation</strong>: To prevent refresh token reuse in your application, implement a mutex/locking mechanism for token refresh operations </div></div></div></div></div><h3 id="body-definition-1" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Body Definition<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#body-definition-1"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h3><section>The following enlists the values that are sent to the Token endpoint to Refreshing Access Tokens:</section><div data-markdown-component="x-tabs-container"><div class="ui-tabs ui-tabs-top ui-tabs-full-content ui-tabs-full-content--scrollable"><div role="tablist" class="ui-tabs-nav"><div class="ui-tabs-nav-wrap" style="flex-grow:1"><div class="ui-tabs-nav-list" style="transform:translate(0px, 0px)"><div data-node-key=".$0" class="ui-tabs-tab ui-tabs-tab-active"><div role="tab" aria-selected="true" class="ui-tabs-tab-btn" tabindex="0">Refresh Access Token Request</div></div><div data-node-key=".$1" class="ui-tabs-tab"><div role="tab" aria-selected="false" class="ui-tabs-tab-btn" tabindex="0">Refresh Access Token Response</div></div><div class="ui-tabs-ink-bar"></div></div></div><div class="ui-tabs-nav-operations aria-controls="null-more-popup" id="null-more" aria-expanded="false"><span role="img" aria-label="ellipsis" class="appicon appicon-ellipsis"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" focusable="false" token<section data-last="true"><br data-first="true"/> <a data-href="https://www.postman.com/salla-app/workspace/salla-e-commerce-platform/request/17687195-852c447f-1cd0-4124-af80-560e41df918d?ctx=documentation" target="_blank"><img class="_cardGroup_o6dzj_70" data-markdown-component="x-card-group" style="grid-template-columns:repeat(2, minmax(0, 1fr))"><h4 id="important-notes" data-first="true" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Important Notes<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#important-notes"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h4><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40"></div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">Refresh tokens expire after 1 month. The latest refresh token must always be used for the next refresh request.Â </span></div></div><div class="_card_o6dzj_12 undefined" data-markdown-component="x-card" data-last="true"><a class="hidden" rel="noreferrer"></a><div class="_cardContainer_o6dzj_61"><div class="_cardTitle_o6dzj_40"></div><span class="_cardContent_o6dzj_49 markdown-child-root">The <code>expires</code> variable</span></div></div></div><h1 id="access-token-usage-example" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">Access Token Usage Example<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#access-token-usage-example"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h1><section>Now you may use the access token to make requests, on behalf of the Merchant, from the resource server via the API <em>(base endpoint url: <span><span class="markdown-child-root _text_6esy6_7"><a href="https://api.salla.dev/admin/v2/" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" data-href="https://api.salla.dev/admin/v2/" target="_blank">https://api.salla.dev/admin/v2/</a></span></span>)</em>. For more information about making API requests, the full API documentation is available <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421117" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421117" target="_blank">here</a>.</section><section>With the access token and the authroized App scopes to the App, you may start consuming any of <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421117" title="" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/doc-421117" target="_blank">Salla&#x27;s API endpoints</a>, such as fetching a list of <a href="https://docs.salla.dev/api-5394213" title="" data-last="true" data-href="https://docs.salla.dev/api-5394213" target="_blank">brands</a></section><section><a href="https://god.gw.postman.com/run-collection/17687195-dc776b52-482b-4dec-ae7b-9659b71a62aa?action=collection%2Ffork&amp;source=rip_markdown&amp;collection-url=entityId%3D17687195-dc776b52-482b-4dec-ae7b-9659b71a62aa%26entityType%3Dcollection%26workspaceId%3D0e589b64-253f-44c2-b947-7508724ec833" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" data-href="https://god.gw.postman.com/run-collection/17687195-dc776b52-482b-4dec-ae7b-9659b71a62aa?action=collection%2Ffork&amp;source=rip_markdown&amp;collection-url=entityId%3D17687195-dc776b52-482b-4dec-ae7b-9659b71a62aa%26entityType%3Dcollection%26workspaceId%3D0e589b64-253f-44c2-b947-7508724ec833" target="_blank"><img src="https://run.pstmn.io/button.svg" alt="Run In Postman" style="width:128px;height:32px" data-first="true" data-last="true" loading="lazy" class=""/></a></section><h1 id="ip-whitelisting" class="markdown-doc-viewer-heading">IP Whitelisting<a class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#ip-whitelisting"><span class="icon-link">#</span></a></h1><section><a href="https://salla.dev/blog/secure-your-apps-with-the-trusted-ip-address-now/" title="" data-first="true" data-href="https://salla.dev/blog/secure-your-apps-with-the-trusted-ip-address-now/" target="_blank">IP whitelisting</a> is a security feature that restricts access to an App to only the IP addresses that are included on the whitelist. This can be used to restrict unwanted access and protect critical data from potential compromise.</section><section>It works by denying all IP addresses, except for those specifically listed as &quot;whitelisted,&quot; thereby limiting the access to only approved users. This way, developers can better protect their private data from potential outside threats, such as hackers and malware, by reducing the attack surface area.</section><section>IP Whitelisting can also be used for other purposes such as controlling bandwidth usage or limiting access to certain services. You may reach the App setup page by going to the Partners Dashboard and selecting the &quot;My Apps&quot; tab:</section><section><img src="https://cdn.salla.network/docs/MerchantAPI/Intro-Auth-02.png" alt="Image1" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" loading="lazy" class=""/></section><section>From this page, you can add the permitted IP addresses in the following area, which is labeled &quot;App Trusted IPs&quot;:</section><section><img src="https://cdn.salla.network/docs/MerchantAPI/Intro-Auth-03.png" alt="image2" title="" data-first="true" data-last="true" loading="lazy"
